MARY'S HOSPITAL 2476170 수술기록 이주희 OBGY (Operation Record) 850410-2****** F/39 진료기간: 2024/10/21 ~ 2024/10/29 주치의: 권지영 병실 : 6-202 수술일자: 2024/10/22 수술과 : 산부인과 [진단명] 수술전 진단명 1. preg 37+2wks c SGA 수술후 진단명 1. preg 37+2wks c SGA [수술명] 1. LCT C/sec (Low cervical transverse cesarean section) [마취종류] D() Regional anesthesia, spinal block 마취종류(부): [수술의사] 집도의: 권지영 보조의: 없음 [수술소견] Baby was out at 2024-10-22 15:07 Single cephalic presentation LF 2.385kg Apgar score (8/9) No gross anomaly. No neck cord coiling. Not meconium stained. Placenta was expelled out by manual traction No defect No calcification. C.Uteri AV, full term size, no myoma Adnexae Grossly normal Intrapelvic cavity: no abonormal fluid accumulated. Other internal organ small amounts of ascites was found No drain, no transfusion during Op. EBL 500cc Under spinal anesthesia Pfannenstiel skin incision Painbuster was inserted [수술과정] The patient was placed in supine position. The skin of the whole abdomen and pubic area were prepared with povidine and sterile drapperies in routine manners. Under spinal anesthesia, the abdomen was opened through Pfannenstiel skin incision which was carried down to peritoneum. Upon the entry of the abdominal cavity, 2 Richardson retractors and long surgical tap were inserted for the bowel preparation and Op field. Then vesicouterine fold was identified. A short transverse incision which was extended in both direction on the lower uterine segment was made with Metzenbaum scissors. Thereafter, the transverse myometrial incision was made on the uterine segment and it was extended laterally by finger traction. Then baby was delivered from the head immediately by gentle guide and extra abdominal compression. The incised corner of the uterus was clamped with sponge forceps. Rapid closure and bleeding control was performed at this space. Endometrium and myometrium was closed in continuous running suture with 1-0 vicryl. Disrupted uterine serosa were repaired by vicryl. And the remaining abdominal wall was closed layer by layer in the routine manner. MARY'S HOSPITAL 2476170 수술기록 이주희 OBGY (Operation Record) 850410-2****** F/39 진료기간: 2024/10/21 ~ 2024/10/29 주치의: 권지영 병실 : 6-202 수술일자: 2024/10/22 수술과 : 산부인과 [진단명] 수술전 진단명 1. preg 37+2wks c SGA 수술후 진단명 1. preg 37+2wks c SGA [수술명] 1. LCT C/sec (Low cervical transverse cesarean section) [마취종류] D() Regional anesthesia, spinal block 마취종류(부): [수술의사] 집도의: 권지영 보조의: 없음 [수술소견] Baby was out at 2024-10-22 15:07 Single cephalic presentation LF 2.385kg Apgar score (8/9) No gross anomaly. No neck cord coiling. Not meconium stained. Placenta was expelled out by manual traction No defect No calcification. C.Uteri AV, full term size, no myoma Adnexae Grossly normal Intrapelvic cavity: no abonormal fluid accumulated. Other internal organ small amounts of ascites was found No drain, no transfusion during Op. EBL 500cc Under spinal anesthesia Pfannenstiel skin incision Painbuster was inserted [수술과정] The patient was placed in supine position. The skin of the whole abdomen and pubic area were prepared with povidine and sterile drapperies in routine manners. Under spinal anesthesia, the abdomen was opened through Pfannenstiel skin incision which was carried down to peritoneum. Upon the entry of the abdominal cavity, 2 Richardson retractors and long surgical tap were inserted for the bowel preparation and Op field. Then vesicouterine fold was identified. A short transverse incision which was extended in both direction on the lower uterine segment was made with Metzenbaum scissors. Thereafter, the transverse myometrial incision was made on the uterine segment and it was extended laterally by finger traction. Then baby was delivered from the head immediately by gentle guide and extra abdominal compression. The incised corner of the uterus was clamped with sponge forceps. Rapid closure and bleeding control was performed at this space. Endometrium and myometrium was closed in continuous running suture with 1-0 vicryl. Disrupted uterine serosa were repaired by vicryl. And the remaining abdominal wall was closed layer by layer in the routine manner. During the operation, the patient was tolerable and sent to the recovery room after operation. 특이사항 및 합병증: No 조직검사: No [추정 출혈량] 500cc 배액: No [입원] 작성자: 권지영 Surgeon : 권지영 페이지: 1/ 1 : 2025/01/07 15:45:33 이미숙 의무기록팀 가톨릭대학교 은평성모병원 THE CATHOLIC UNIV.
